\DoxyCodeLine{00727\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ N\ =\ ceil\ (\ pi\ /\ acos(1\ -\/\ error\ /\ r)\ )\ \ \ \ \ where\ r\ >\ 0,\ error\ <=\ r}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00730\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ will\ get\ this\ result.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00731\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00733\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ asymmetrical\ results\ on\ the\ raster\ grid.\ Therefore\ we're\ rounding\ N\ to\ next\ even\ number\ (7-\/>8,\ 8-\/>8,\ 9-\/>10\ etc.)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{01399\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Routing\ policies\ for\ Shortcut()\ +\ low-\/level\ SetShortcutRouting()}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01400\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ The\ general\ idea\ is\ that\ several\ callers\ register\ interest\ in\ a\ shortcut,\ and\ only\ one\ owner\ gets\ it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01401\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ -\/\ When\ a\ policy\ (other\ than\ \_RouteAlways)\ is\ set,\ Shortcut()\ will\ register\ itself\ with\ SetShortcutRouting(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01402\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ allowing\ the\ system\ to\ decide\ where\ to\ route\ the\ input\ among\ other\ route-\/aware\ calls.}}
